< Review>
My family has been using Banfield for all of our pets for the past 15+ years and I started bringing my own puppy recently, however I can't be loyal if the service is continuously subpar.

It has now happened three times where I arrive to the appointment and call for a check-in, however no one responds. The first two times, someone finally picked up after 15 or so minutes and they were able to take my dog. Frustrating but passable. This last time I sat for 30 minutes calling to check-in and when they finally picked up, they let me know that I had missed my dog's appointment. They acknowledged that they couldn't pick up the phone because there was only one person available to answer and that there were many calls, therefore my call went unanswered.

Instead of fitting my dog in, they asked me to drop her off for a 6pm pickup when her appointment was at 10:30am. So I left my puppy, who had only had breakfast, through 6pm, having her miss two meals. This was the only option they gave me and said they would give her "a treat". No idea whether they did or not.

I think the vets at this location have been knowledgeable but the service isn't worth continuing to be a loyal customer. There are plenty of great vets with better service for customers. Definitely take your pet somewhere that can provide the support and professionalism you're expecting so your time taken off from work is met with the same respect you have given by being on time -- you won't consistently find that here.</Review>

I moved in on the 2nd of the month, when I was rained out of my apartment they did the new lease start date on the 9th of the month, (without my consent), and when I gave my move out notice for the 9th, they told me I had to make it for the 11th, (because they don't do move outs on the weekend, thus, making me pay an additional 2 days.) I gave them back their keys on Saturday, the 9th, but I had paid through the 11th of the month. I am lividly angry with the management because I have NEVER been a problem tenant, and I even tried to roll with the punches when a lot of my personal property was severely damaged or destroyed when THEIR apartment flooded during the rains, and I was displaced for days. Their apartments are outdated, (except for the few that they have recently updated since my 1st apartment flooded), and this complex is well overpriced! <user>105882274058396270172<//user><user_name>ImagesByChaos Tee</user_name><date>1523662889438<//date><Rating>5</Rating><Text>While no management company can predict how a tenant will be 100%, the current staff here has done a great job of assuring that we have great neighbors with respect for the community and for others who share their space.  The occasional bad neighbor is always something that happens when you are apartment living, but the RP team seems to have managed to keep that to a minimum.

They have a great Maint staff that does all they can to keep a very aging property, vibrant and alive with quick turnarounds on reported issues and pretty solid grounds keeping in general.  RP may not have all the most modern amenities in the units, but they are by no means falling apart or in bad repair.  I constantly see the staff here working to improve the property and maintain it while still offering a fairly reasonable (for a beach city in Southern California) rent rate.

The staff is friendly and go out of their way to know their residents, especially those who go out of their way to help build those relationships.  You cannot force people to be open and understanding, but the demeanor of the staff here, enables those who choose to have those connections with staff, are enabled to do so.

My wife an I have happily lived here for almost 6 years now, in several units, 1 and 2 bdrm, and have been very happy since day one, but never more than we are with the current staff!

No apartment complex is perfect and nowhere will ever have 100% satisfaction with all of our neighbors, there are just too many personalities in the world for that, but RP does a pretty good job of building a friendly and safe community for it's residents...with very few exceptions in our experience!

<time>1409159972267</time><Rating>2</Rating><text>We absolutely love our new apartment in the Regency Palms Apartment community. We had our reservations at first, concerned about living alongside so many others in this 310 unit complex. We were assured that we would be happy, but if for any reason we decided it wasn't going to workout for us, we were given a 30-day satisfaction period from our move in date to change to another available unit OR to move out, No Harm No Foul, should we decide. Well, needless to say, we are VERY happy and wish to stay for a very long time
.
This IS a dog friendly community, but we ourselves are NOT dog owners. Regardless, they are no bother, but instead a joy to watch...and play with when the opportunity arises. There are green belts all through the complex so whether it's to walk your dog or just for taking an evening stroll with your loved ones, the grounds here at the Regency Palms have beautiful , well-kept landscaping and big beautiful trees to offer shade on those hot summer days. There are Doggy Waste Stations strategically placed all through the complex to help keep the grassy areas as clean and sanitary as possible. I see the Orkin man here every week inspecting and treating all areas and issues that may cause a problem if gone unattended. Due to there diligent and professional work, this community is bug free. I haven't seen one critter in over 2-months.

The Leasing Office Staff, including their maintenance and cleaning crews, have been an absolute blast to deal with. I've had a service request or two that I needed assistance with. Once reported to the Leasing Team, our issues were quickly and efficiently dealt with keeping me a happy & content camper :) Their five (5) laundry room facilities are always clean and available. The washers are bigger and less expensive than the Laundromat across the street in the shopping center. Trust me, we've checked. And speaking of local shopping & recreation, the Regency Palms is located within walking distance from grocery stores, Home Depot and lots of other much needed services. Very convenient! It's a miles walk to the Library, Central Park, AND Goldenwest College, and not to forget the Westminster Mall.
I have made some good friends already and all the people who live here are very nice. One of my favorite things to do here on a hot day is to go lay out, get wet and socialize poolside, in any one of their 3-well maintained pools + Jacuzzi. When I'm out enjoying the pool area, It's just like being at a Palm Springs resort.

In closing, let me just say this.........."If you are looking for a great place to live and  haven't checked out The Regency Palms yet, What Are You Waiting For?" Call and set up an appointment for a tour by one of their fantastic Leasing Agents. I promise , You WON'T be let down! :)))</text><pictures>None<//pictures>< resp>

Update 8/29/18:  In addition to concerns I note below about Zum's operations, parents should be aware that several 5 star reviews here were posted by individuals who appear to be employed by Zum based on Linkedin profiles, including:  Matthew Meyer, Martin Veliz, and Pedro Silva. If Zum's employees are posting employees of the company without disclosing their affiliation/connection to the company, that is misleading and deceptive as well as a violation of Google's policy (conflict of interest).

Original review:  Unsafe, unreliable, poor customer service--my son's school has been using Zum for school transportation for several months and our experience has been very poor. On multiple occasions, drivers have taken unsafe (unlit, windy, narrow) routes in the dark, engaged in unsafe loading/unloading practices, and have left students behind.  Zum's management/founders have also been unresponsive, dismissive, and unprofessional in response to complaints and feedback.  I am aware of at least one other Bay Area school that has experienced similar issues.  I do not believe Zum is ready to take on the responsibilities and care that is needed when transporting young children.  Zum and similar companies like it need to be better regulated. Please beware of Zum's terms of service--which purport to disclaim liability for anything that might go wrong--e.g., accidents, injuries, death. Zum also does not warrant their background checks of drivers. These terms are completely inconsistent with Zum's  promises to provide parents with peace of mind.< /review>

< review>
I went to the New Chick-fil-A a day after the opening because I wanted to avoid the high traffic. I skipped the drive thru and went inside to get my meal. It took me from parking to walking out with food in hand about 20-25mins.

I got the:
#2 deluxe meal with lemonade, 12ct nuggets, Peach Milkshake (~$22 dollars)

I used the restaurant WiFi to help use my time there.

Place was packed!

I will return.

Certainly this restaurant will serve the local community (Victorville, Apple Valley, Hesperia, Adelanto, Barstow, Oak Hills, etc) very well!

Edit: some other reviews about the long line, I have been in the High Desert since 2016 and have waited for a Chick-fil-A for 5 years now and we got one.< /review>

<rating>5<//rating><review>As a retired system engineer, I spent a week coming up to speed on HVAC systems. I also spent 2 weeks getting 9 bids, which is over kill for most people; but the installer is the most important part of having a new system installed.  I read 100s of reviews many of which were from people who had no clue if their system was installed correctly, only that it looked nice and the installers were courteous. If the units are installed wrong, it could be years before you might find out that they were installed wrong.  So, when Shawn came out, I asked many detailed questions, such as, vapor/suction line size, flushing procedure for removing the R22 to replace with R410, how they keep the inside of the copper lines clean when cutting them, the evacuation procedure, etc.  Shawn not only had knowledgeable answers, but loved talking about it. He described in detail what they would do on the installation. Additionally, I needed an extension plenum to handle all my ducts and 90 degrees return plenum to relief the bend in my return air.  He also wrote down in detail what would be done, including all the addition materials that would be required to compete the job. I said that I wanted the part numbers of the AC unit, the furnace, and the evaporator coil on the quote; many bids came back with nomenclature, but no actual part numbers. I guess you are supposed to just trust them.  I told him I would be checking the serial numbers of the units to ensure they were manufactured recently. I‚Äôm a trust but verify type of guy.
